279‚Üí      });\n   280‚Üí    }\n   281‚Üí  }, []);\n   282‚Üí\n   283‚Üí  // Callback to sync instance changes from persistence layer\n   284‚Üí  const updateInstanceForPersistence = \n   290‚Üí    isSaving, \n   291‚Üí    lastSaved, \n   292‚Üí    saveError, \n   293‚Üí    documentId,\n   294‚Üí    saveDocument \n   295‚Üí  } = useDocumentPersistence({\n   296‚Üí    instance,\n   297‚Üí    updateInstance: updateInstanceForPersistence,\n   298‚Üí  });\n   299‚Üí\n   300‚Üí  const updateStageState = useCallback((stageId: string, updates: Partial<StageState>) => {\n   301‚Üí    let needsImmediateSave = false;\n   302‚Üí    const resultState = setInstance(prevInstance => {\n   303‚Üí      const newStageStates = {\n   304‚Üí        ...prevInstance.stageStates,\n   305‚Üí        [stageId]: {\n   306‚Üí          ...prevInstance.stageStates[stageId],\n   307‚Üí          ...updates,\n   308‚Üí        },\n   309‚Üí      };\n   310‚Üí      // Decide persistence before returning 321‚Üí\n   322‚Üí    if (needsImmediateSave) {\n   323‚Üí      // Next tick save so React state has committed\n   324‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {\n   325‚Üí        saveDocument();\n   326‚Üí      }, 0);\n   327‚Üí    }\n   328‚Üí  }, [saveDocument]);\n   329‚Üí\n   330‚Üí  // Enhanced dependency evaluation logic with support for autoRunConditions\n   331‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   332‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   333‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   334‚Üí\n   335‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   336‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   337‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   338‚Üí\n   339‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   340‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   341‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   342‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   343‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   344‚Üí        );\n   345‚Üí      }\n   346‚Üí\n   347‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   348‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   349‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   350‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   351‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   352‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   353‚Üí          );\n   354‚Üí        }\n   355‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   356‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   357‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   358‚Üí          );\n   359‚Üí        }\n   360‚Üí      }\n   361‚Üí      \n   362‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   363‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   364‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   365‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   366‚Üí        \n   367‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   368‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   369‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   370‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   371‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   372‚Üí          });\n   373‚Üí        }\n   374‚Üí        \n   375‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   376‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   377‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   378‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   379‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   380‚Üí          });\n   381‚Üí        }\n   382‚Üí        \n   383‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   384‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   385‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   386‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   387‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   388‚Üí          });\n   389‚Üí        }\n   390‚Üí      }\n   391‚Üí\n   392‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   393‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   394‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   395‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   396‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   397‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   398‚Üí        );\n   399‚Üí      } else {\n   400‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   401‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   402‚Üí      }\n   403‚Üí\n   404‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   405‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   406‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   407‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   408‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   409‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   410‚Üí        } else {\n   411‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   412‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   413‚Üí        }\n   414‚Üí      }\n   415‚Üí\n   416‚Üí      if (\n   417‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   418‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   419‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   420‚Üí      ) {\n   421‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   422‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   423‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   424‚Üí Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   433‚Üí  };\n   434‚Üí  \n   435‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   436‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   437‚Üí 441‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   442‚Üí\n   443‚Üí\n   444‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   445‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   446‚Üí }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   455‚Üí\n   456‚Üí\n   457‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   458‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n Try refreshing the page.\",\n    88‚Üí        isTemplate: false\n    89‚Üí      };\n    90‚Üí    }\n    91‚Üí    if (error.includes('Network') || error.includes('fetch')) {\n    92‚Üí      return {\n    93‚Üí        message: \"Network error: Unable to connect to the AI service. It allows developers to:\n\n- View components in isolation\n- Test different component states and props\n- Generate automatic documentation from JSDoc comments\n- Provide interactive examples for the design system\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Installation\n\nThe necessary Storybook dependencies are included in the project's `package.json`. To install them:\n\n```bash\nnpm install\n```\n\n### Running Storybook\n\nStart the Storybook development server:\n\n```bash\nnpm run storybook\n```\n\nThis will start Storybook on `http://localhost:6006`.\n\n### Building Storybook\n\nTo build a static version of Storybook for deployment:\n\n```bash\nnpm run build-storybook\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Main Configuration (`main.ts`)\n\n- **Stories**: Automatically discovers `.stories.@(js|jsx|mjs|ts|tsx)` files in the `src` directory\n- **Addons**: Includes essential addons for documentation, interactions, and controls\n- **Framework**: Configured for Next.js with TypeScript support\n- **Autodocs**: Automatically generates documentation pages for tagged stories\n\n### Preview Configuration (`preview.ts`)\n\n- **Global Styles**: Imports the project's global CSS (Tailwind)\n- **Controls**: Configures automatic prop detection for color and date types\n- **Actions**: Sets up action logging for event handlers\n\n## Writing Stories\n\n### Basic Story Structure\n\n```typescript\nimport type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react';\nimport { YourComponent } from './your-component';\n\nconst meta = {\n  title: 'Category/YourComponent',\n  component: YourComponent,\n  parameters: {\n    layout: 'centered',\n  },\n  tags: ['autodocs'],\n  argTypes: {\n    // Configure controls for props\n  },\n} satisfies Meta<typeof YourComponent>;\n\nexport default meta;\ntype Story = StoryObj<typeof meta>;\n\nexport const Default: Story = {\n  args: {\n    // Default props\n  },\n};\n```\n\n### Best Practices\n\n1. **Categorization**: Use logical categories in the `title` field:\n   - `UI/ComponentName` for basic UI components\n   - `Wizard/ComponentName` for wizard-specific components\n   - `Layout/ComponentName` for layout components\n\n2. **Documentation**: Include JSDoc comments on components and props for automatic documentation generation\n\n3. **Story Variants**: Create stories for different states:\n   - Default state\n   - Loading state\n   - Error state\n   - Different variants/sizes\n   - Real-world usage examples\n\n4. **Controls**: Configure `argTypes` to provide interactive controls for component props\n\n## Component Categories\n\n### UI Components (`src/components/ui/`)\n\nBasic design system components:\n- **Button**: All button variants with different states\n- **Card**: Card layouts and compositions\n- **Badge**: Status and informational badges\n- **Alert**: Alert messages and notifications\n\n### Wizard Components (`src/components/wizard/`)\n\nWorkflow-specific components:\n- **WizardShell**: Main orchestration component\n- **StageCard**: Individual workflow stage\n- **StageInputArea**: Input handling for stages\n- **StageOutputArea**: Output rendering for stages\n\n### Layout Components (`src/components/layout/`)\n\nApplication layout and navigation:\n- **MainNav**: Primary navigation\n- **SiteHeader**: Application header\n- **SiteFooter**: Application footer\n\n## Design System Integration\n\nThe Storybook setup is designed to work seamlessly with the project's design system:\n\n- **Tailwind CSS**: Full Tailwind support with project configuration\n- **shadcn/ui**: All shadcn/ui components are documented\n- **Design Tokens**: Color system and spacing are reflected in stories\n- **Typography**: Font choices (Space Grotesk for headlines) are preserved\n\n## Deployment\n\nFor production deployment, build the static Storybook and serve the files:\n\n```bash\nnpm run build-storybook\n# Serve the storybook-static directory\n```\n\n## Contributing\n\nWhen adding new components:\n\n1. Test different component states and edge cases\n5.
